Although performed often play, ostensible equality women men modern-day society justifies every recurrence. The recent iteration “Little Women” hit Chicago area presented First Folio Theatre Mayslake Peabody Estate Oak Brook. After twenty-six years, founding executive director David Rice retiring closing company, making “Little Women” third-to-last production final season. The lives four March sisters framed dark mahogany wood beams numerous nooks filled bursting books spacious attic. Jo (Shelby Lynn Bias) independent, voracious reader aspiring writer. Oldest sister Meg (Stephanie Fongheiser) Jo’s near-opposite, content marry become housewife. Third-oldest Beth (Jamie Herb) resembles Dickensian heroine—subdued, angelic, trying please everyone—too good world. The youngest sister, Amy (Esther Fishbein), brat, grows become mature-ish artist. Each personality trait amplified maximum, making girls appear childish ages—Amy, twelve years old, comes across seven eight, developmental drop afflicts characters. But chemistry feels right, interactions, though highly animated, come genuine heartfelt. Jamie Herb (Laurie) Esther Fishbein (Amy) First Folio Theatre’s “Little Women”/Photo: Tom McGrath The actors perform double duty, everyone except Bias playing sister male love interest. Fishbein briefly steps shoes Meg’s future husband, John Brooke, Fongheiser manages German-ish accent Professor Bhaer. Herb plays Laurie, Jo’s eager, wide-eyed childhood boyfriend, not-so-secretly pines throughout friendship. Among fans ongoing debate whether Jo married Laurie not. This production unambiguous asserting Jo would never happy immature whiny partner, winds falling older Professor Bhaer. Two visual metaphors used great effect. While Paris, Amy uses inflatable red balloons symbolize art, releasing every work deems masterpiece sent squealing twisting air. In brilliant scene production, new housewife Meg loses mind attempting make currant jam, lightweight juggling scarves representing many things “up air.” Director Melanie Keller moves show along quick pace keeps viewer enthralled. The adaptation, written Heather Chrisler, contains big twists Alcott would approve of. Today, phrase “what woman” slur used men television politics denigrate others. The women “Little Women,” defined clearly First Folio Theatre’s recent production, show womanhood exists spectrum. It’s sad we—mostly men—need reminder, works like important, performers audiences return again. “Little Women” First Folio Theatre Company Mayslake Peabody Estate, 1717 31st Street Oak Brook, firstfolio.org, (630)986-8067. Tickets $49-$59 discounts seniors students. Sarawak 29 Dec 2022 Bersatu asks Dewan Rakyat Speaker vacate four seats GRS KUALA LUMPUR: The insurance protection scheme housewives available Dec 1, says Datuk Seri M. Saravanan. The Human Resources Minister said scheme cover homemakers injuries suffered tending chores would managed Social Security Organisation (Socso). For now, provides coverage housewives, added. ‘’I call husbands fathers come forward, sign start contributing. This show love care,’’ said press conference yesterday. On July 26, Dewan Rakyat passed Housewives Social Security Bill (HSS), allows husbands voluntarily contribute scheme wives age 55. The scheme offers insurance coverage RM300 RM50,000, depending seriousness injuries sustained. Asked definition housewife would widened cover husbands assume role homemakers well, Saravanan said ministry would need in-depth study see number house husbands involved. “If need arises, ministry problem extend coverage male homemakers too,’’ said. Saravanan said HSS scheme voluntary husbands compelled make contributions wives. “No action would taken husband contribute.” However, noted husbands signed contribute failed maintain monthly would fined RM10,000. “Those signed face problems contribute later discuss file application Socso. “For example, maybe lost source income divorce took place, come forward within 60 days exempted,” said. Saravanan also said amendments passed Employment Insurance System Act 2017 (Act 800) Employees’ Social Security Act 1969 (Act 4) increase maximum monthly salary ceiling limit RM4,000 RM5,000 would come effect next month. “This improve social security coverage workers’ protection,” said, adding worker’s highest lowest contribution RM7 70 sen month. With ceiling limit changed since 2016, said amendments would see workers receiving wider protection benefits, especially cost living gone up. The increase would involve, among others, temporary disability benefits, permanent disability benefits, disability pensions retirement pensions. It started 40 years ago, letter paper led register bored women stuck home suburbia. And now? Raekha Prasad Mon 28 Feb 2000 23.50 GMT * * * It sharp frustration dollop sympathy Guardian journalist Betty Jerman wrote surburbia 40 years ago. The open space fresh air, said, made good place bring children, feared advantages outweighed brain-numbing atmosphere. "Surburbia incredibly dull place live I blame women," wrote. "They stay day. They set tone. Many look back regret days worked office. Their work kept alert. Home childminding blunting effect woman's mind. But sharpen it." Jerman's observations struck chord reader Maureen Nicol. She wrote paper suggesting "housebound wives liberal interests desire remain individuals could form national register, whenever one moves, one contact like-minded friends". An avalanche letters sent paper desperate women country felt floundering society expected wives mothers. Women educated but, like mothers them, found trapped domestic sphere, often sticks husband's job, even they'd found kindred spirit nearby. Local groups formed years later acquired name National Housewives' Register. In absence personal income, early members admit fiddling housekeeping raise small membership fee. Today groups meet every week discuss everything except domestic, debates current affairs, book groups speakers invited every public sphere. Year year membership grew until, 1980, peaked 24,000. This enthusiasm proved Virginia Woolf right when, A Room Of One's Own, wrote: "Women sat indoors millions years, time walls permeated creative force, has, indeed, overcharged capacity bricks mortar must needs harness pens brushes business politics." Numbers falling since 80s; today 8,000 women members known since 1987 National Women's Register. The change title raises question organisation's future. The oldest member 92 though members late 20s, generation women means rushing join. NWR may celebrating ruby anniversary organisation born alleviate lot housewife survive drink golden when, politically personally, apparently dead buried? Imagine outcry Tony Blair made example housewife's foresight way Margaret Thatcher did. The title banished social history archives rears head unreconstructed genres TV quiz shows market research questionnaires. The spic 'n' span 50s feather duster image British housewife went Hilda Ogden Ken Dodd. Instead, debate women domesticity evolved anxiety keeping house bringing children. So whereas better "him" woman stay home, argument best kids. The observation Jerman made mental "pay-off' housewife makes still echoes. What's best children may what's best modern woman. The lack status implied prefix "just" housewife died term attaches word mother. "Working mother" rolls tongue ease "housewife" did. These women longer go voluntary exile marry children but, argues Mary Dodkins, NWR's marketing co-ordinator, still need space someone's wife mother, place opinionated without fear consequences. Today, members work, rules extended - discussion domestic still stands jobs out-of-bounds subject. "The purpose meetings still stimulate grey cells," Dodkins says. "Many women feel limited job position. It place feel real thoughts said, controversial discussions are, better." For Kathryn de Motte, 37 youngest area organiser 30-strong NWR group Nottingham, emphasis speaking mind crucial. She works secretary finds opinions says articulate anywhere else."We different hats," explains. "I'm mother, I'm wife I work, there's never space me. We get together exercise diet open minds." De Motte speaks enthusiastically subjects speakers discussions introduced her: badgers, local history learning juggle lighter end; Kafka, fox-hunting infant mortality rates serious. But women juggle domestic work, need NWR? "It's still important like-minded women," de Motte says. "Women still pressures men. In husband's life, strongest role job, I role wife mother. We need space us - without children." Time home, alone, without chores, still often felt shirking responsibility. De Motte, example, attend NWR meetings husband away employing babysitter would "leave guilt-ridden". So although women define paid job, often definition addition to, instead of, domestic labour. Pauline Reymond, long-time NWR member regional organiser Worthing, joined group 29 child started school. Now 64, notes members "partners" well husbands many divorced, widowed remarried. Her life goes way explaining how, term "housewife" made redundant social forces, also created them. Reymond give job secretary Royal Exchange Insurance company employ married women. "It way things were," says. Though Reymond would leave job today, things changed: matter call them, still women housework. The last Office National Statistics figures showed that, £739bn, unpaid housework worth value formal economy. And domesticity still hard work. The best outcome hope for, far NWR goes, continue fall victim success. Hebburn News The Hebburn housewife battled decades pollution local cokeworks A new book, Clean Air, recalls Tyneside housewife Jennie Shearan united local community fight pollution neighbourhood forced endure nechronicle * Bookmark * Share * * * * * Comments News By David MortonNostalgia Editor * 16:00, 3 OCT 2022 Bookmark Hebburn Residents’ Action Group, Jennie Shearan, Monkton Cokeworks behind, 1980s, book Clean Air Hebburn Residents’ Action Group, Jennie Shearan, Monkton Cokeworks behind, 1980s, book Clean Air (Image: Gianfranco Rosolia) Get latest South Tyneside news updates delivered straight inbox ____________________Invalid emailSomething went wrong, please try later. We newsletters Show MeNo thanks, close See Privacy Notice The construction Monkton Cokeworks outskirts Hebburn mid 1930s well-intentioned project. Built former farmland, sprawling complex provided work hundreds men time mass unemployment Great Depression wreaked economic havoc around world, especially Tyneside spawned 1936 Jarrow Crusade. But time, plant became universally regarded giant blot landscape, pumping continuous smoke grime becoming major environmental health issue lived nearby. A newly-published book, Clean Air , tells story rise everyday housewife Jennie Shearan campaigning environmentalist. It written grandson, Gianfranco Rosolia, born raised Tyneside, currently lives Los Angeles. READ MORE:Then Now: Newcastle City Hall 1973 - iconic venue today Clean Air relates story people lived doorstep Monkton Cokeworks 1953 1990. Their daily reality nightmare hazardous acrid sulphur dioxide emissions, all-pervading soot, clamorous noisy tannoys. Over decades, facility grew unflaggingly, converting ever-increasing quantities coal coke without concern residents’ well-being. In forming Hebburn Residents’ Action Group, Jennie Shearan brought together underrepresented residents Monkton Lane Estate, gave voice, igniting national dialogue health risks pollution neighbourhood endure. The view Monkton Cokeworks Hebburn Jennie Shearanʼs home, 1980s, book Clean Air The view Monkton Cokeworks Hebburn Jennie Shearanʼs home, 1980s, book Clean Air (Image: Gianfranco Rosolia) While events book took place South Tyneside 30 years ago, remains resonance challenges Jennie Shearan overcome campaign environmental justice. She battled negligent big energy firm prioritised profit people, governmental bodies lacked accountability, institutional sexism. She took levels establishment, British Coal Margaret Thatcherʼs government, galvanising underrepresented town bringing case way European Parliament. Jennie’s grandson, author Clean Air , Gianfranco Rosolia, says: “Throughout arduous journey, Jennie brave, steadfast sincere, demonstrating level resourcefulness tenacity would inspire leader, capacity corral group around single-minded vision politician could learn from, degree resilience energise us all. The book Clean Air, Hebburn campaigner Jennie Shearan Her Majestyʼs Inspectorate Pollution, 1980s The book Clean Air, Hebburn campaigner Jennie Shearan Her Majestyʼs Inspectorate Pollution, 1980s (Image: Gianfranco Rosolia) “The book illustrates countless sacrifices bold choices Jennie made, effectiveness grassroots activism people power, beauty leaving behind better world future generations. Jennie Shearan Hebburn Residents’ Action Group deeply loved community. They put heart spirit improving lives ordinary people. Their redoubtable efforts left deeply positive long-lasting legacy, giving thousands people hope stronger healthier future transforming quality life. "To continue good work, proceeds CLEAN AIR go directly three charities represent Jennie fighting for: Hebburn Helps , Friends Earth , The Environmental Law Foundation .” The book received praise notable supporters, including Geordie rock star Sting said: “This inspirational story female empowerment, grassroots activism environmental justice. What eloquent spokesperson Jennie Shearan was.” Monkton Cokeworks finally closed 1990 demolished two years later. Three decades on, area reclaimed pleasant green space, paths popular walkers cyclists. Jennie Shearer died aged 82 2005. FALSE: Solo parents, mothers, housewives given P10,000 monthly allowance Facebook Twitter (BUTTON) Share article Copy URL Copied As July 2022, announcements national government government agencies regarding At glance * Claim: The government distributing monthly cash aid amounting P10,000 solo parents, mothers, housewives. * Rating: FALSE * The facts: As writing, announcements national government regarding this. * Why fact checked this: The video containing claim reached 71,000 reactions Facebook. Complete details Since July 13, video circulating Facebook containing claim solo parents, mothers, housewives given P10,000 monthly allowance government. This false. As July 2022, announcements national government regarding this. There also new reports local governments government agencies regarding monthly allowance given groups. Last June, Expanded Solo Parents Welfare Act Republic Act No. 11861 lapsed law. The law includes new provisions distribution P1,000 cash subsidy solo parents whose income poverty line 20% discount infant formula, diapers, medicines, vaccines, necessities. March 19, 2021 Opinion Working woman versus Housewife Money reason choose working wife Rayees Ahmad Kumar By Rayees Ahmad Kumar 1585 0 Facebook Twitter Linkedin WhatsApp Email The common misunderstanding among people, especially among materialistic approach, lady working government department, private company multinational corporation regarded working woman, whereas lady isn’t working departments companies, household tasks dusk dawn tirelessly like cooking, washing, taking care children many jobs, called non-working woman housewife. Can call lady drawing monthly salary working woman one making life easy, comfortable pleasant non-working woman? No absolutely never. If make review daily routine needs home run smoothly, come conclusion woman made run smoothly utmost success. - Advertisement - After man completed education also got good job public private sector, next priority always marry good girl. Among many criteria fixed intending grooms choosing woman wife, one important whether marry working woman stay-at-home housewife. His choice, wish parents opinion close friends colleagues directly impact final decision marrying working woman stay-at-home housewife. It undoubtedly said rising inflation skyrocketing prices essentials, becoming expensive passing day, compelling today’s youth look match working woman, certainly reasons also prefer working woman non-working one. Sometimes government employee officer government department regards insult choose non-working woman finds friends colleagues marrying working women. Living luxurious life, better standard life maximising one’s desires forcing almost every individual seek ways good income available means. Marrying working woman one means increase one’s income meet one’s expenses. However also good percentage people who, despite government service, prefer marry non-working woman. For reasons aspirations. For good service home living comfortable stress-free life, prefer nonworking woman staying home. Though time wedding choosing one’a life partner, one feels delighted working woman partner time things make one realize hasn’t taken good decision. In joint family, often situation takes ugly turn mostly couple feel worried working daughter in-law doesn’t receive good cooperation husband’s parents in-laws. When lunch, dinner two times tea husband in-laws gets late due known reasons daughter in-law, everybody family gets worried sometimes force daughter in-law say goodbye service. Due over-busy schedule, working couple faces many problems issues home well outside home. There common saying “money can’t buy everything”, working couple materialistic mind, intent making wealth gathering luxuries life, always find lamenting end. A working woman may able manage children way be. After coming back school children find alone house wait hours together parents, personality isn’t developed properly parents’, especially mother’s, love, affection presence must early years child’s growth development. The strong humanistic fabric family gets altogether shattered parents, children siblings don’t get required time expressing problems issues discussing proper way family member doesn’t feel alienated. At many instances found aged ailing parents working couple either found dead rooms without noticed family member taken hospitals people duty-bound so. The social life working couple gets affected due over-busy schedule. They can’t reach loved ones, near dear ones relatives specific occasions. - Advertisement - Due over-busy schedule, working couple faces many problems issues home well outside home. There common saying “money can’t buy everything”, working couple materialistic mind, intent making wealth gathering luxuries life, always find lamenting end. On hand stay-at-home housewife, always serves husband utmost care honesty, takes care husband’s ailing aged parents manages children true spirit mother, regarded successful woman outside family. A non-working lady best serve husband, manage home social life remains intact. The family members home, neighbours relatives unanimously praise extraordinary skills shows managing home taking care every aspect family life. One important aspect working women often become victims depression mental trauma non-working counterparts often live happy, prosperous contended life. Web Series + Weird * GRUB * Outdoors * Earworm Gender Dispelling Myth Housewife Who “Sits Home Does Nothing” housewife [pinit_fg_en_rect_gray_20.png] Illustration: Arati Gujar * * * * * * * By Huzan Tata Mar. 08, 2020 Let’s proud women making life decisions free will, whether choose fly plane 30,000 feet sea level run home way wish. They never needed permission anyway. My mother urban woman English-medium education. She Bachelors Master’s degrees Arts, voracious reader. She’s never shied away speaking mind almost never politically correct. The word “diplomatic” doesn’t exist mother’s dictionary. She wears whatever likes whenever likes, others’ opinions damned. She stands ground arguments matter who’s end, seldom puts people’s nonsense (she gives back equal measure), always self-assured woman. She’s one confident people I’ve ever known, forever comfortable 61-year-old skin. My mother also housewife choice, one since day got married. Surprised? More often not, think housewives around us – whether mothers, grandmothers, aunts neighbours – though cut domesticated cloth. Many millennial generation think cater husbands, houses, kids, otherwise “do nothing all”. Even movies grew show homemakers in-law-worshipping, always submissive husbands families, weak, rarely opinionated strong personalities, personality all. Thanks, Bollywood. But can’t showcase, okay with, badass women choosing housewives? I’ve asked mom many occasions, like tend question homemakers, whether she’s ever dreamt pursuing career income. “Do think brought money? I provided everything else,” comes proud response. My mother perfectly happy provider everything apart salary – ambition mother, every time kids needed her. She work got married, first teaching kindergarten desk job while, never developed liking work life. She’s never regretted choice, let anyone make feel ashamed guilty it. And shouldn’t either. What’s home? Till brother I almost adults, didn’t driver, cook, full-time domestic help. It mom – like countless homemakers – travelled BEST buses drop fetch us birthday parties swimming classes, walked bazaars stock kitchen cook meals, helped homework whenever needed, attended PTA meetings, accompanied us doctor, cared us sick. And still made time – read, beloved newspaper crosswords sudokus, meet friends, shop, write daily diary, whatever else wanted. If women choose housewives truly owning it, look them? From young age, brother I taught independent self-reliant, mom forcing travel alone bus age 10 I didn’t need fetch friends’ houses. She stayed sibling fights “because need learn deal problems yourself”, made brother several household chores (PSA: kids “free house help” middle-class families). She taught fill pass books rounds banks financial work pre-netbanking era. I could go questions I boys, periods, sex, everything else sun, even got little weird. And matter many times I asked she’d ever great ambitions outside four walls home, one answer: happiest homemaker, qualms wearing badge pride. If women choose housewives truly owning it, look them? We shame kind choosing “sit home nothing” (have ever seen housewife’s schedule?), assume she’s confined home life outside factors – qualifications finding job, family objections she’s unambitious. Why can’t treat homemakers around us respect give CEO who’s killing boardroom lawyer spends hours poring case files? There though, say housewife thankless unpaid job, express gratitude ladies spend days home, everything us. But need respect one gives career-woman choices makes – isn’t feminism about? Let’s proud women making life decisions free will, whether choose fly plane 30,000 feet sea level run home way wish. They never needed permission anyway. At least mom doesn’t. By Samantha Kamman, Christian Post Reporter Housewife, baking Getty Images A TikTok trend stay-at-home moms sharing daily routine performing domestic work prompted debate whether encourages women submissive. As Insider reported earlier month, women showcasing lives homemakers part trend American women making “trad wife” (traditional wife) content showing positive aspects housewife. The trad wife hashtag 96 million views TikTok, users incorporating usernames. Estee C. Williams, 24-year-old creates content TikTok, defines trad wife woman “who chooses live traditional life ultra-traditional gender roles." Williams lives Virginia husband, Conner. In June, homemaker posted video listing things make life enjoyable, including listening music cleaning, wearing makeup cute house dresses, taking candle-lit baths. In interview Insider, Williams said disparaging women’s right work, adds housewives like believe many “women drifted far [our] roots.” "For me, hustle culture appealing. Being wife, mom, making delicious home-cooked meals family, keeping warm, inviting home truly spoke me,” Williams said. The social media influencer added working good women, fears many workforce suffer burnout. "I choose promote lifestyle showcase fulfillment lifestyle gives,” said. According 2020 analysis conducted Great Place Work healthcare start-up Maven, mothers paid employment 23% likely experience burnout fathers paid employment. The study surveyed 1,200 U.S. companies 400,000 working parents. The analysis included 226,000 working mothers 204,000 working fathers, respond 60 questions Great Place Work’s Trust Index survey. An estimated 2.35 million working mothers U.S. suffered burnout start COVID-19 pandemic, mainly “due unequal demands home work,” according study. Another survey conducted business networking site LinkedIn assessed nearly 5,000 members site July 31 Aug. 13 last year. The study found working women men face similar stresses, intensity level always higher women. Seventy-four percent women said felt “very somewhat stressed” work-related reasons, compared 64% working men. Forty percent working women cited “not enough time day get everything done” one top stress factors, versus 35% male respondents. The Insider report noted trad wives believe feminism persuaded women enter workforce instead full-time wives mothers. Deborah Etienne, Brandwatch data analyst researcher tracking social media trend, asserted "many trad wives reject feminism, claiming destroyed everything." Whitman College sociologist Michelle Janning told Insider chaos pandemic might influenced women full-time stay-at-home mothers. According Janning, stress working outside home time might led women decide home best option. "As sociologist, I would say, people collectively feel like there's lot control world, cling something familiar, concrete might comfortable," told Insider. Janning also cautioned trad wives creating content promote homemaking healthy lifestyle. She claimed might use trend champion "conservative white supremacist views." Another TikTok user identified trad wife, Madison Dastrup, stopped associating term September reason. The sociologist added women TikTok actually pursuing career “outside home” working social media influencers. "It could they're selling product selling version themselves, husband getting sponsorship,” Janning said. “It's contradiction: job tell people job." She went insinuate society’s “gender system” tells women homemaker lifestyle choice, it’s really pushing toward role full-time housewife. "It's less choice maybe think is,” Janning said. Abby Roth, conservative host "Classically Abby" podcast, promotes classic feminist values, examined #TradWide trend May 2020 article Evie. Roth claimed versions trend “demean women” instead merely celebrating stay-at-home moms. Some definitions trend, Roth explained, claim women traditional stay home full-time. “A classic woman traditional wife mother even work knows passion work support traditional life home,” wrote. “Where feminism proposes women actively choose career family, classic says work family go hand-in-hand.” The feminist emphasized husband wife must commit growing alongside one another, encouraging become better versions themselves. She argued #Trad trend appears discourage women speaking husbands improve character. “Because #Trad definition expects wives submissive husbands dominant, creates inherent power imbalance relationship,” Roth wrote time. She asserted marriages “should based partnership, subservience.” According YouGov survey Institute Family Studies/Wheatley Institution 2,500 American adults, ages 18-55, conducted May 28 June 10 last year, 53% parents children younger 18 prefer working home time half time due pandemic. Sixty-five percent college-educated fathers supported idea working home least half time time. Approximately 44% supported working home time, 21% support working home half time. Among college-educated mothers, 57% endorse shift. Mothers likely fathers voice preference flexible work hours sharing childcare responsibilities partners. Nearly 30% moms dads believe one parent staying home full-time “best arrangement” children 5. The researchers behind survey concluded results support idea parents caring children work arrangement allows it. Samantha Kamman reporter The Christian Post. According several media reports, spike divorce cases seen days COVID-19 pandemic lockdown. Especially women, mostly financially reliant caring someone else's family long time. This family long time, start identify part eventually lose sense self. Based Oakley’s PhD research, pioneering feminist book looks role housewife modern industrialised society. “The study domestic labour taken seriously — wasn’t understood topic, fact,” Oakley tells sit office Institute Education London professor sociology social policy. During research, Oakley, 70, interviewed 40 women living suburban London. She found tended dissatisfied monotony, fragmentation social isolation inherent role housewife. Therefore, “housework directly opposed possibility human self-actualisation,” concluded call abolish housewife role. “I deliberately provocative,” explains book’s final chapter also called abolition traditional family abolition traditional gender roles. Four decades later, what’s changed? “I think whole notion women housewives changed,” replies. “If asked women talk housewives wouldn’t know talking really.” But concedes men housework today, explains it’s still equal. “I don’t think study world shows it’s equal.” Sure enough, newly published 2014 Global Trends survey, 70 per cent British women said mostly responsible cooking, food shopping household cleaning. These findings supported research Organisation Economic Co-operation Development (2013) Institute Public Policy Research (2012), show British women still lion’s share domestic labour. “Most change happened since ’70s been, view, fairly superficial,” Oakley says. “The change behaviour probably less professed attitude — people say egalitarian do.” In particular, Oakley’s 1970s research interested inequality responsibility. “In far men housework construed men women helping housework — way round. “In terms issue responsibility, happened 1970s still happening now.” When men pitch in, studies show generally end tasks arguably enjoyable leisurely — gardening DIY, example. Oakley agrees. “In area childcare, it’s still case men likely enjoyable side childcare, rather changing dirty nappies.” So grossly unfair status quo continue? “Patriarchy simple explanation,” Oakley argues. “Men privileged group reason give privilege unless forced so.” This feminism comes in. “Most change men’s behaviour, I suspect, come women involved put pressure change. Men haven’t, en masse, decided housework good thing do.” Oakley sees increasing men’s involvement housework childcare important step addressing social problem masculinity — topic explored 2011 Guardian article co-written fellow feminist academic Cynthia Cockburn. Quoting government statistics, noted: “Men perpetrators 91 per cent violent incidents England Wales … 81 per cent domestic violence, 86 per cent assault, 94 per cent wounding, 96 per cent mugging, 98 per cent robbery.” In addition, Ministry Justice figures show men responsible 98 per cent sexual offences, 92 per cent drug offences 89 per cent criminal damage. “The evidence involved basic care work, involved close relationships dependent people including children, something brings qualities traditionally associated woman — caring, altruism that,” Oakley says. “That happens men too, first willing put position changes occur.” According 2011 research Churchill Home Insurers, one seven population pay outside hired help housework. Oakley doesn’t buy solution problem. “That’s solution often people hired women underpaid, job conditions security good,” says. “And usually woman household responsible looking hired help. So you’ve simply passed oppression sense.” Oakley’s politics research interests energised second-wave feminism early 1970s. Forty years later, many commentators argue currently midst fourth-wave feminism, groups campaigns UK Feminista, Everyday Sexism No More Page 3 evidence renewed feminist activism. “I don’t know enough really,” Oakley admits I ask resurgent movement. However, feels media discussions around contemporary feminism aware little common women’s liberation movement ’70s. She points current focus representation women positions power. “We arguing women’s share top jobs. We talking basic issues, arguing level basic reproductive rights access childcare — state-provided childcare. It something domestic oppression undoing privilege top.” Rather getting bigger portion pie, argues, “it changing pie. We wanted different kind pie.” She philosophical I suggest work, work many feminists generation, rarely cited popular feminist polemics published today. “Time moves — it’s one sad things much rediscovered time again,” says. In fact says found one book referred dead — “The late Ann Oakley.” “I’m late sense I’m dead also I’m quite punctual person,” quips. Having read Housewife Oakley’s stupendously good Gender Planet Earth — book moves men meat-eating critiquing post-modernism — I safely say contemporary feminism missing lot ignoring Oakley’s groundbreaking work. As recent surveys mentioned show, housework continues source inequality men women. Housewife could therefore key text revival feminist concern housework must take place women gain semblance equality future. Ian Sinclair author The March That Shook Blair: An Oral History 15 February 2003, published Peace News Press. He tweets @IanJSinclair.
